   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function(){
 			if(typeof window.screen.width != 'undefined' && window.screen.width < 1050)
 			{
 				$('#site_zoom_overlay').show();
 			}
 			else
 			{
 				$('#site_zoom_overlay').hide();
 			}
 			
 			var currFFZoom = 1;
 			var currIEZoom = 100;
 			
 			$('#site_zoom_plus').on('click',function()
 			{
 				if(navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Firefox") > -1)
 				{
 					var step = 0.02;
 					currFFZoom += step; 
 					$('body').not('#site_zoom_overlay').css('MozTransform', 'scale(' + currFFZoom + ')');
 					$('#site_zoom_overlay').css({
 						'MozTransform': 'scale('+ ((currFFZoom <= 1) ? 1+(1 % currFFZoom) : 1-(currFFZoom % 1)) +')'
 					});
 					$('body').css({
 						'marginTop': (currFFZoom >= 1) ? Math.abs($('body').position().top) + 'px' : '-' + Math.abs($('body').position().top) + 'px'
 					});
 				}
 				else
 				{
 					var step = 2;
 					currIEZoom += step;
 					$('body').not('#site_zoom_overlay').css('zoom', ' ' + currIEZoom + '%');
 					if(navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Chrome') > -1)
 					{
 						$('#site_zoom_overlay').css({
 							'zoom': ((currIEZoom <= 100) ? 100+(100 % currIEZoom) : 100-(currIEZoom % 100)) +'%'
 						});
 					}
 				}
 			});
 			
 			$('#site_zoom_minus').on('click',function()
 			{
 				if(navigator.userAgent.indexOf("Firefox") > -1)
 				{
 					var step = 0.02;
 					currFFZoom -= step;                 
 					$('body').not('#site_zoom_overlay').css('MozTransform', 'scale(' + currFFZoom + ')');
 					$('#site_zoom_overlay').css({
 						'MozTransform': 'scale('+ ((currFFZoom <= 1) ? 1+(1 % currFFZoom) : 1-(currFFZoom % 1)) +')'
 					});
 					$('body').css({
 						'marginTop': (currFFZoom >= 1) ? Math.abs($('body').position().top) + 'px' : '-' + Math.abs($('body').position().top) + 'px'
 					});
 				}
 				else
 				{
 					var step = 2;
 					currIEZoom -= step;
 					$('body').not('#site_zoom_overlay').css('zoom', ' ' + currIEZoom + '%');
 					if(navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Chrome') > -1)
 					{				
 						$('#site_zoom_overlay').css({
 							'zoom': ((currIEZoom <= 100) ? 100+(100 % currIEZoom) : 100-(currIEZoom % 100)) +'%'
 						});
 					}
 				}
 			});
 		});
   </script>

              <script>
               function toggleFreeMenue()
 {
     var freemenue = $('.freemenue_content'),
         freemenue_show_all = $('.freemenue_show_all'),
         count_all = freemenue.length,
         limit = 20;
 
     limit = (limit > count_all) ? count_all : limit;
     
     if(freemenue.is(':hidden'))
     {
         freemenue.show();
         freemenue_show_all.hide();
     }
     else
     {
         freemenue_show_all.show();
         freemenue.each(function(i){
             $(this).hide();
             if(i < limit)
             {
                 $(this).show();
             }
         });
     }
 }
 $(document).ready(function(){
     toggleFreeMenue();  
 });
              </script>
